class is the foundation of Django's CSRF protection. Key implementation details:\\n\\n1. **Token Validation Chain**: The process_view method initiates validation, calling _check_token which:\\n   - Retrieves the CSRF secret from cookies or sessions via _get_secret\\n   - Extracts the request token from POST data or HTTP headers\\n   - Validates token format using _check_token_format\\n   - Compares tokens using _does_token_match, which calls constant_time_compare for timing-attack-safe comparison\\n\\n2. **Token Masking (BREACH Protection)**: \\n   - _mask_cipher_secret: Creates a masked token by combining a random mask with the secret using XOR-like operations\\n   - _unmask_cipher_token: Recovers the original secret from a masked token\\n   - Tokens are masked when sent to clients but unmasked for comparison\\n\\n3. **Origin and Referer Validation**:\\n   - _origin_verified: Validates Origin headers against CSRF_TRUSTED_ORIGINS\\n   - _check_referer: Strict referer checking for HTTPS requests\\n   - Both methods prevent cross-domain attacks\\n\\n4. **Timing-Attack Prevention**:\\n   - _does_token_match (line 143-157) uses constant_time_compare from django.utils.crypto\\n   - This prevents attackers from using timing differences to guess valid tokens\\n\\n## CSRF Decorators (django/views/decorators/csrf.py)\\nProvides view-level CSRF protection without middleware:\\n- csrf_protect: Wraps CsrfViewMiddleware for individual views\\n- csrf_exempt: Marks views exempt from CSRF checks\\n- requires_csrf_token: Ensures token availability without enforcement\\n- ensure_csrf_cookie: Guarantees CSRF cookie is set in response\\n\\n## Timing-Attack-Safe Comparison (django/utils/crypto.py)\\nThe constant_time_compare function (line 65-67) uses secrets.compare_digest to prevent timing attacks. This is critical because:\\n- Compares tokens in constant time regardless of where they differ\\n- Prevents attackers from determining token validity through timing analysis\\n- Used exclusively in _does_token_match for token validation\\n\\n## Template Integration\\n1. **CsrfTokenNode (django/template/defaulttags.py)**:\\n   - Implements {% csrf_token %} template tag\\n   - Renders hidden input field with masked token\\n   - Retrieves token from template context (csrf_token variable)\\n\\n2. **Context Processors (django/template/context_processors.py)**:\\n   - csrf function provides csrf_token to RequestContext\\n   - Lazily evaluates get_token to avoid unnecessary computation\\n\\n3. **Lazy Utilities (django/template/backends/utils.py)**:\\n   - csrf_token_lazy: Lazily evaluates get_token\\n   - csrf_input_lazy: Lazily renders complete hidden input field\\n   - Supports both Django templates and Jinja2\\n\\n## CSRF Failure Handling (django/views/csrf.py)\\nThe csrf_failure view handles rejected requests:\\n- Displays informative error page when CSRF validation fails\\n- Configurable via CSRF_FAILURE_VIEW setting\\n- Provides debugging information in DEBUG mode\\n- Includes specific messages for different failure reasons (missing cookie, missing referer, etc.)\\n\\n## Security Checks (django/core/checks/security/csrf.py)\\nPerforms configuration validation:\\n- check_csrf_middleware: Warns if CsrfViewMiddleware not enabled\\n- check_csrf_cookie_secure: Warns if CSRF_COOKIE_SECURE not set to True\\n- check_csrf_failure_view: Validates CSRF failure view signature and importability\\n\\n## Complete Validation Chain\\nRequest → CsrfViewMiddleware.process_view() → _check_token() → _get_secret() → _check_token_format() → _does_token_match() → constant_time_compare() → Accept/Reject → csrf_failure() (on rejection)\\n\\nAlternatively, with decorators:\\nRequest → csrf_protect decorator → CsrfViewMiddleware logic (same as above)\\n\\nToken rendering flow:\\nTemplate → {% csrf_token %} → CsrfTokenNode.render() → csrf context processor → get_token() → _mask_cipher_secret() → HTML output\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1195,"cache_read_input_tokens":80014,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1195},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5abd30f6-f642-4221-aacb-c603584ebd61","uuid":"b3d48409-0cb1-4d2d-a2f8-c58655939712"}

class is the foundation of Django's CSRF protection. Key implementation details:\\n\\n1. **Token Validation Chain**: The process_view method initiates validation, calling _check_token which:\\n   - Retrieves the CSRF secret from cookies or sessions via _get_secret\\n   - Extracts the request token from POST data or HTTP headers\\n   - Validates token format using _check_token_format\\n   - Compares tokens using _does_token_match, which calls constant_time_compare for timing-attack-safe comparison\\n\\n2. **Token Masking (BREACH Protection)**: \\n   - _mask_cipher_secret: Creates a masked token by combining a random mask with the secret using XOR-like operations\\n   - _unmask_cipher_token: Recovers the original secret from a masked token\\n   - Tokens are masked when sent to clients but unmasked for comparison\\n\\n3. **Origin and Referer Validation**:\\n   - _origin_verified: Validates Origin headers against CSRF_TRUSTED_ORIGINS\\n   - _check_referer: Strict referer checking for HTTPS requests\\n   - Both methods prevent cross-domain attacks\\n\\n4. **Timing-Attack Prevention**:\\n   - _does_token_match (line 143-157) uses constant_time_compare from django.utils.crypto\\n   - This prevents attackers from using timing differences to guess valid tokens\\n\\n## CSRF Decorators (django/views/decorators/csrf.py)\\nProvides view-level CSRF protection without middleware:\\n- csrf_protect: Wraps CsrfViewMiddleware for individual views\\n- csrf_exempt: Marks views exempt from CSRF checks\\n- requires_csrf_token: Ensures token availability without enforcement\\n- ensure_csrf_cookie: Guarantees CSRF cookie is set in response\\n\\n## Timing-Attack-Safe Comparison (django/utils/crypto.py)\\nThe constant_time_compare function (line 65-67) uses secrets.compare_digest to prevent timing attacks.
